<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/colla#English" title="colla">colla</a></span> (<i>Bermuda</i>), <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/colour#English" title="colour">colour</a></span> (<i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Nations" class="extiw" title="w:Commonwealth of Nations">Commonwealth</a>, Ireland</i>) (see the <a href="#Usage_notes">usage notes</a> below)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/colour#Middle_English" title="colour">colour</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/color#Middle_English" title="color">color</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/colur#Old_French" title="colur">colur</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/colour#Old_French" title="colour">colour</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/color#Old_French" title="color">color</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/color#Latin" title="color">color</a></i>. Displaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blee#English" title="blee">blee</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/blee#Middle_English" title="blee">blee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">color</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/bleo#Old_English" title="bleo">blƒìo</a></i>. Also partially replaced <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/hiew#Old_English" title="hiew">hƒ´ew</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">color</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and its descendants, which is less often used in this sense. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/couleur#English" title="couleur">couleur</a></i>.
</p><p>In the US, the spelling <i>color</i> is used to match the spelling of the word's Latin etymon<span class="serial-comma">,</span> and to make all derivatives consistent (<i>colorimeter</i>,  <i>coloration</i>, <i>colorize</i>, <i>colorless</i>, etc). Elsewhere in the English-speaking world, the spelling <i>colour</i> has been retained.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">k≈≠l π…ôr</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/Ààk ål.…ö/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">k≈≠l π…ôr</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/Ààk ål.…ô(…π)/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">color</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/colors#English" title="colors">colors</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(Canadian spelling, rare)</i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The spectral composition of visible light.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Humans and birds can perceive <b>color</b>.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blee#English" title="blee">blee</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A subset thereof:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A particular set of visible spectral compositions, perceived or named as a class.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Most languages have names for the <b>colors</b> black, white, red, and green.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blee#English" title="blee">blee</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hue#English" title="hue">hue</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1918</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/W._B._Maxwell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:W. B. Maxwell">W. B. Maxwell</a>,  chapter 5, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1097634W">The Mirror and the Lamp</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Here, in the transept and choir, where the service was being held, one was conscious every moment of an increasing brightness; <b>colours</b> glowing vividly beneath the circular chandeliers, and the rows of small lights on the choristers' desks flashed and sparkled in front of the boys' faces, deep linen collars, and red neckbands.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/hue" title="hue">Hue</a> as opposed to <a href="/wiki/achromatic" title="achromatic">achromatic</a> colors (black, white and grays).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He referred to the white flag as one "drained of all <b>color</b>".</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hue#English" title="hue">hue</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/shade#English" title="shade">shade</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blee#English" title="blee">blee</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>These hues as used in <a href="/wiki/color_television" title="color television">color television</a> or films, color photographs, etc (as opposed to the shades of grey used in black-and-white television).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">This film is broadcast in <b>color</b>. &nbsp;Most people dream in <b>color</b>, but some dream in black and white.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/color_television#English" title="color television">color television</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/heraldry" title="heraldry">heraldry</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the standard dark <a href="/wiki/tincture" title="tincture">tinctures</a> used in a <a href="/wiki/coat_of_arms" title="coat of arms">coat of arms</a>, including <a href="/wiki/azure" title="azure">azure</a>, <a href="/wiki/gules" title="gules">gules</a>, <a href="/wiki/sable" title="sable">sable</a>, and <a href="/wiki/vert" title="vert">vert</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms coordinate-term"><span class="defdate">Coordinate terms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/metal#English" title="metal">metal</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/stain#English" title="stain">stain</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/paint" title="paint">paint</a>.
<dl><dd><i>The artist took out her <b>colors</b> and began work on a landscape.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Human skin tone, especially as an indicator of race or <a href="/wiki/ethnicity" title="ethnicity">ethnicity</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Color</b> has been a sensitive issue in many societies.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/complexion#English" title="complexion">complexion</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ethnicity#English" title="ethnicity">ethnicity</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/race#English" title="race">race</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/medicine" title="medicine">medicine</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Skin color, noted as normal, <a href="/wiki/jaundiced" title="jaundiced">jaundiced</a>, <a href="/wiki/cyanotic" title="cyanotic">cyanotic</a>, <a href="/wiki/flush" title="flush">flush</a>, <a href="/wiki/mottled" title="mottled">mottled</a>, <a href="/wiki/pale" title="pale">pale</a>, or <a href="/wiki/ashen" title="ashen">ashen</a> as part of the <a href="/wiki/skin_signs" title="skin signs">skin signs</a> assessment.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/flushed" title="flushed">flushed</a> appearance of blood in the face; redness of complexion.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1864</b>, Sir Henry Stewart Cunningham, <i>Late Laurels</i> (volumes 1-2, page 117)
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>‚Ä¶<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> her very embarrassment wore a graceful air; her high <b>colour</b> had softened down to a warm, delicate tint; and her dress, which looked beautifully new and fresh, was in good taste, and showed her off to advantage.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Richness of expression; detail or flavour that is likely to generate interest or enjoyment.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><i>There is a great deal of <b>colour</b> in his writing.</i></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">a bit of local <b>color</b></i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1914</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Joseph_Vance" class="extiw" title="w:Louis Joseph Vance">Louis Joseph Vance</a>,  chapter I, in  <cite>Nobody</cite>, New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_H._Doran_Company" class="extiw" title="w:George H. Doran Company">George H[enry] Doran Company</a>, published 1915, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/40817384">40817384</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Three chairs of the steamer type, all maimed, comprised the furniture of this roof-garden, with (by way of local <b>colour</b>) on one of the copings a row of four red clay flower-pots filled with sun-baked dust<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>‚Ä¶<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Could you give me some <b>color</b> with regards to which products made up the mix of revenue for this quarter?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/standard" title="standard">standard</a>, <a href="/wiki/flag" title="flag">flag</a>, or <a href="/wiki/insignia" title="insignia">insignia</a>:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/standard" title="standard">standard</a> or <a href="/wiki/banner" title="banner">banner</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The loss of their <b>colors</b> destroyed the regiment's morale.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/banner#English" title="banner">banner</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/standard#English" title="standard">standard</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The flag of a nation or team.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The <b>colors</b> were raised over the new territory.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Gang insignia.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Both of the perpetrators were wearing <b>colors</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An award for sporting achievement, particularly within a school or university.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He was awarded <b>colors</b> for his football.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/military" title="military">military</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The morning ceremony of raising the flag.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/physics" title="physics">physics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A property of <a href="/wiki/quark" title="quark">quarks</a>, with three values called red, green, and blue, which they can <a href="/wiki/exchange" title="exchange">exchange</a> by passing <a href="/wiki/gluon" title="gluon">gluons</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/finance#Noun" title="finance">finance</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/w/index.php?title=third-order&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="third-order (page does not exist)">third-order</a> measure of <a href="/wiki/derivative" title="derivative">derivative</a> price sensitivity, expressed as the rate of change of <a href="/wiki/gamma" title="gamma">gamma</a> with respect to time, or equivalently the rate of change of <a href="/wiki/charm" title="charm">charm</a> with respect to changes in the <a href="/wiki/underlying" title="underlying">underlying</a> <a href="/wiki/asset" title="asset">asset</a> <a href="/wiki/price" title="price">price</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/typography" title="typography">typography</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The relative <a href="/wiki/lightness" title="lightness">lightness</a> or <a href="/wiki/darkness" title="darkness">darkness</a> of a mass of written or printed <a href="/wiki/text" title="text">text</a> on a page. (See <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/type_color" title="w:type color"><img alt="Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/15px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/23px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/30px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></a> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/type_color" class="extiw" title="w:type color">type color</a></b> on  Wikipedia.<span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/type_color" class="extiw" title="w:type color">Wikipedia </a></span>.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/snooker#Noun" title="snooker">snooker</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the colored balls excluding the <a href="/wiki/red" title="red">reds</a>.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/front" title="front">front</a> or <a href="/wiki/facade" title="facade">facade</a>; an <a href="/wiki/ostensible" title="ostensible">ostensible</a> truth actually false; <a href="/wiki/pretext" title="pretext">pretext</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2011</b>, David Baldacci, <i>The Collectors</i>
<dl><dd>At the far end of the continuum, Roger Seagraves collected personal items from people he'd murdered, or assassinated rather, since he'd done it under the <b>color</b> of serving his country.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>An appearance of right or authority; <a href="/wiki/color_of_law" title="color of law">color of law</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;‚ñº</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Under <b>color</b> of law, he managed to bilk taxpayers of millions of dollars.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1882</b>, <i>The Ohio Law Journal</i> (volume 2, page 396)
<dl><dd>The only thing which this defendant is accused of doing is that he excluded this boy from the school, and he did it under the <b>color</b> of the statute relating to the subject, and did it because he was a colored boy.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/colour#Old_French" title="colour">colour</a></i>, which is the standard UK spelling, has been the usual spelling in Britain since the 14th century and was chosen by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Johnson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Johnson">Dr. Johnson's</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Dictionary_of_the_English_Language" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Dictionary of the English Language">Dictionary of the English Language</a></i> (1755) along with other Anglo-Norman spellings such as <a href="/wiki/favour" title="favour">favour</a>, <a href="/wiki/honour" title="honour">honour</a>, etc. The Latin spelling <i>color</i> was occasionally used from the 15th century onward, mainly due to Latin influence; it was lemmatized by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Noah_Webster" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Noah Webster">Webster's</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Webster%27s_Dictionary" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Webster's Dictionary">American Dictionary of the English Language</a></i> (1828), along with <a href="/wiki/favor" title="favor">favor</a>, <a href="/wiki/honor" title="honor">honor</a>, etc., and is currently the standard US spelling.
</p><p>In Canada, <i>colour</i> is preferred, but <i>color</i> is not unknown; in Australia, <i>-our</i> endings are the standard, although <i>-or</i> endings had some currency in the past and are still sporadically found in some regions. In New Zealand and South Africa, <i>-our</i> endings are the standard.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">color</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Conveying color, as opposed to shades of gray.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Color</b> television and movies were considered a great improvement over black and white.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">color</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/colors#English" title="colors">colors</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/coloring#English" title="coloring">coloring</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/colored#English" title="colored">colored</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To give something color.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/dye#English" title="dye">dye</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/paint#English" title="paint">paint</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/stain#English" title="stain">stain</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/shade#English" title="shade">shade</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/tinge#English" title="tinge">tinge</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/tint#English" title="tint">tint</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We could <b>color</b> the walls red.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause (a pipe, especially a <a href="/wiki/meerschaum" title="meerschaum">meerschaum</a>) to take on a brown or black color, by smoking.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To apply colors to the areas within the boundaries of a line drawing using colored markers or crayons.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/color_in#English" title="color in">color in</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">My kindergartener loves to <b>color</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a person or their face</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become red through increased blood flow.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blush#English" title="blush">blush</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Her face <b>colored</b> as she realized her mistake.</i></div></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></li>
<li>To affect without completely changing.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/affect#English" title="affect">affect</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/influence#English" title="influence">influence</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That interpretation certainly <b>colors</b> my perception of the book.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To attribute a quality to; to portray (as).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/call#English" title="call">call</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Color</b> me confused.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They tried to <b>colour</b> the industrial unrest as a merely local matter.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mathematics" title="mathematics">mathematics</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/graph_theory" title="graph theory">graph theory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/assign" title="assign">assign</a> colors to the <a href="/wiki/vertex" title="vertex">vertices</a> of a <a href="/wiki/graph" title="graph">graph</a> (<i>or</i> the <a href="/wiki/region" title="region">regions</a> of a <a href="/wiki/map" title="map">map</a>) so that no two vertices connected by an <a href="/wiki/edge" title="edge">edge</a> (regions sharing a border) have the <a href="/wiki/same" title="same">same</a> color.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Can this graph be 2-<b>colored</b>?</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You can <b>color</b> any map with four colors.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Galician">Galician</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Galician">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_3">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="gl"><a href="/wiki/cor#Galician" title="cor">cor</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From Old Galician and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician-Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:Galician-Portuguese">Old Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href="/wiki/color#Old_Portuguese" title="color">color</a></i>, alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href="/wiki/coor#Old_Portuguese" title="coor">coor</a></i>, perhaps from an older forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt">collor</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asturian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Asturian language">Asturian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ast"><a href="/wiki/collor#Asturian" title="collor">collor</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="ast"><a href="/wiki/color#Asturian" title="color">color</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/color#Latin" title="color">color, col≈çrem</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_10">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp"><a href="/wiki/color#Old_Spanish" title="color">color</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/colorem#Latin" title="colorem">col≈çrem</a></i>, singular <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#accusative_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">accusative</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/color#Latin" title="color">color</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=color&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="es">color</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-es p-form-of" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/colores#Spanish" title="colores">colores</a></b>)
